The overall scale of the hot spring center is relatively small. It is said that there is an outdoor part, which may not be open to the public in winter.
Service: The staff are friendly and patient.
This time I stayed in a sea view room with a very large sea view balcony. Overall it was a good experience and suitable for a family vacation. I hope to experience it again in the summer if I have time.
